The English sentence is in the first person singular (I) and uses the auxiliary verb "want" followed by an infinitive verb (to help). To translate this idea into Spanish, we use "tranquilizarte," which comes from "tranquilo/a," meaning calm, and "te" (reflexive pronoun for "you"). <NL> 3. So, the final translation is: "Quiero ayudarte a tranquilizarte."
